-- Yes, high chairs (the wooden kind, 3 or 4, see picture).
-- Bar height order/payment counter can be a put-off for wheelchair bound patrons.
-- Small dining/waiting/ordering area completely taken up by one side being a long, shared table, and the other side two bar-height tables (see pictures). < Text>
Really fast, really good pizza.
Really affordable compared to most other pizzerias.

1st visit pizzas ordered:
~Cheese pizza - average cheese pie for the kiddos, hard to go wrong but still better than those Hot & Ready places.  CHEAPER as well!!

~White garlic chicken & sausage with artichoke.  I practically ate half in-store and the other half the next day.  Light crust, just enough flavor but not overpowering or salty.  Not soggy despite the cheese and garlic sauce.  SO MUCH TOPPINGS...every bite had some of the toppings.

I most likely wouldn't bring the kids to this general area to eat at night but Delish Pizza will most certainly be my #1 choice for pizza pickups on the way home from work.< /Text>

<Review>Forrest R.

I went online looking for a new pizza establishment and stumbled upon
Delish. I checked their menu out and decided to give them a try. When I called, the staff was very friendly and professional. I ordered a large combo, the price and delivery charge was much lower than I expected, compared to other pizza places in my area.

Bought two brown rocker-recliners around Thanksgiving, "Ashley" furniture. The floor model felt great and comfortable. The two recliners were delivered in less than a week, and set up in my home by the delivery team. < Review>
The service needs a lot of work.  It's a new restaurant so maybe they'll work out the kinks.  The food is reasonably good, not great, but probably a little above average for North County Thai (no a high barrier).   Service, on the other hand not great.  I had two issues:
First, my wife's entree came out about 10 minutes after mine... no big deal.
More significantly, I ordered the roasted duck curry; when they brought my entree, it was the honey roasted duck, which had no type of sauce or anything particularly Thai about it, just a roasted duck and not what I had in mind.    When they brought it out, I told the runner that wasn't my dish.   The server came over, said let me check and showed me her iPad and said, see, it says honey duck, not curry.  I told her no matter what her iPad said, that wasn't what I ordered.
I said I would take the honey roasted duck, as we were going to the movies and didn't have time to have another entree made.   She apologized, but there was no accommodation made as would be in a restaurant with well trained staff or systems; a free drink or desert, an offer for a price reduction or offer to expedite a new order.
Hopefully they'll get their act together; it's nice to have a Thai place nearby, but based on first impressions.....< /Review>

<Date>1485080063484<//Date><pics>None<//pics><Text>A great team that offers excellent service.

Detail of Experience:

I had my crown done by Dr. Espinosa in one appointment.  I didn't need to come for a temporary crown, schedule another appointment for the permanent crown, or come back when the measurements are wrong.  Dr. Espinosa prepared my tooth for a crown, measured it, built my crown on site (while the hygienist was cleaning the rest of my teeth), and placed my permanent-great-quality-crown, ALL-IN-ONE-SEATING!

Price:

I thought it was pricey when Jessica (the office manager/receptionist) gave me the estimate for the work they needed to do, so, I went to another dental office that was highly recommended by my coworker.  I wanted to see if I can find a better price and to get a second opinion if I really needed to get the work done.  My coworker's dental office quoted me a similar price for the same work but with less quality materials. Plus, it would have taken multiple appointments because they are not as high tech as Bonita Del Rey Dental Care.

Additional Comments:

I've moved quite a bit in the past so I've been to more than a few dental offices.  I can honestly say that by far, Bonita Del Rey Dental Care is the best one I've been to. I've been going to them for four (4) years now.  Out of all the visits I've had, it was only one (1) time when I waited for more than 15 minutes to be seen; and that was because they had an emergency procedure.

Regardless of how excellent this team of professionals are, I still get nervous going to the dentist!!! üôÄüôä #scradeycat< /Text></record></dataset><record>
